they
call
the
white
emir
the
blond
assassin
and
spy
skilled
in
combat
and
sorcery
who
moves
adeptly
and
lethally
through
the
worlds
of
both
east
and
west
against
him
stands
simon
de
gobignon
a
proud
young
nobleman
from
one
of
the
great
and
accursed
houses
of
france
each
fights
gallantly
and
desperately
for
the
civilization
he
serves
and
for
the
love
of
the
ravishing
sophia
whose
powerful
erotic
allure
no
other
mortal
woman
can
surpass
and
no
man
alive
can
resist
